id: the numeric identity being evaluated\n//   - policyName: the name or key of the policy\n//   - verdict: the policy verdict (allow or deny)\n//   - reason: the reason for the verdict\nfunc (pal *PolicyAuditLogger) LogDecision(id identity.NumericIdentity, policyName string, verdict PolicyVerdict, reason string) {\n\tpal.mu.Lock()\n\tdefer pal.mu.Unlock()\n\n\tscopedLog := log.WithFields(logrus.Fields{\n\t\tlogfields.Identity: id,\n\t\t\"policyName\":       policyName,\n\t\t\"verdict\":          string(verdict),\n\t\t\"reason\":           reason,\n\t})\n\n\tswitch verdict {\n\tcase PolicyVerdictAllow:\n\t\tscopedLog.Debug(\"policy audit: allow decision\")\n\tcase PolicyVerdictDeny:\n\t\tscopedLog.Debug(\"policy audit: deny decision\")\n\tdefault:\n\t\tscopedLog.Debug(\"policy audit: decision\")\n\t}\n\n\t// Also log to the audit logger's own output if configured\n\tpal.logger.WithFields(logrus.Fields{\n\t\tlogfields.Identity: id,\n\t\t\"policyName\":       policyName,\n\t\t\"verdict\":          string(verdict),\n\t\t\"reason\":           reason,\n\t}).Info(\"policy audit decision\")\n}\n\n// LogEvaluation logs a full policy evaluation event including selector cache\n// interaction results.\n// Parameters:\n//   - id: the numeric identity being evaluated\n//   - policyName: the name or key of the policy\n//   - verdict: the policy verdict (allow or deny)\n//   - reason: the reason for the verdict\nfunc (pal *PolicyAuditLogger) LogDecision(id identity.NumericIdentity, policyName string, verdict PolicyVerdict, reason string) {\n\tpal.mu.Lock()\n\tdefer pal.mu.Unlock()\n\n\tscopedLog := log.WithFields(logrus.Fields{\n\t\tlogfields.Identity: id,\n\t\t\"policyName\":       policyName,\n\t\t\"verdict\":          string(verdict),\n\t\t\"reason\":           reason,\n\t})\n\n\tswitch verdict {\n\tcase PolicyVerdictAllow:\n\t\tscopedLog.Debug(\"policy audit: allow decision\")\n\tcase PolicyVerdictDeny:\n\t\tscopedLog.Debug(\"policy audit: deny decision\")\n\tdefault:\n\t\tscopedLog.Debug(\"policy audit: decision\")\n\t}\n\n\t// Also log to the audit logger's own output if configured\n\tpal.logger.WithFields(logrus.Fields{\n\t\tlogfields.Identity: id,\n\t\t\"policyName\":       policyName,\n\t\t\"verdict\":          string(verdict),\n\t\t\"reason\":           reason,\n\t}).Info(\"policy audit decision\")\n}\n\n// LogEvaluation logs a full policy evaluation event including selector cache\n// interaction results.\n// Parameters:\n//   - ctx: context for the evaluation\n//   - policyKey: a string key identifying the policy being evaluated\n//   - selectorCache: the SelectorCache used during evaluation\n//   - result: a string describing the evaluation result\nfunc (pal *PolicyAuditLogger) LogEvaluation(ctx context.Context, policyKey string, selectorCache *SelectorCache, result string) {\n\tpal.mu.Lock()\n\tdefer pal.mu.Unlock()\n\n\tfields := logrus.Fields{\n\t\tlogfields.PolicyKey: policyKey,\n\t\t\"result\":            result,\n\t}\n\tif selectorCache != nil {\n\t\tselectorModel := selectorCache.GetModel()\n\t\tfields[\"selectorCount\"] = len(selectorModel)\n\t}\n\n\tscopedLog := log.WithFields(fields)\n\tscopedLog.Debug(\"policy audit: evaluation\")\n\n\tpal.logger.WithFields(fields).Info(\"policy audit evaluation\")\n}\n\n// SetLevel sets the log level for the audit logger.\nfunc (pal *PolicyAuditLogger) SetLevel(level logrus.Level) {\n\tpal.mu.Lock()\n\tdefer pal.mu.Unlock()\n\tpal.logLevel = level\n\tpal.logger.SetLevel(level)\n}\n\n// GetLevel returns the current log level of the audit logger.\nfunc (pal *PolicyAuditLogger) GetLevel() logrus.Level {\n\tpal.mu.Lock()\n\tdefer pal.mu.Unlock()\n\treturn pal.logLevel\n}\n","numLines":127,"startLine":1,"totalLines":127}}}
